				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Wer mich liebet, der wird mein Wort halten, BWV 59 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1723/24 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="18 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voices_and_chorus_with_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voices and chorus with orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>For Whit Sunday.
</p>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<ol><li>Duetto (Soprano, Bass): Wer mich liebet, der wird mein Wort halten. This setting proves Bach “to be a master even in limitation”<sup>1</sup>. Derived from brief motives, this duet is highly concentrated in material but very beautiful. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Soprano): O, was sind das vor Ehren. Recitative with string accompaniment. 
</li><li>Chorale: Komm, Heiliger Geist, Herre Gott. A plain chorale setting. 
</li><li>Aria (Bass): Die Welt mit allen Königreichen. An aria in <i>Bar</i> form with obbligato violin. At the end of the bass part, there is marked <i>Choral Segue,</i> a confusing remark that may explain the “missing” movement. 
</li></ol>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Print_Sources_Consulted">Print Sources Consulted</span></h4>
<ul><li>Dürr, Alfred. <i><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://astore.amazon.com/intemusiscorl-20/detail/0199297762/">The Cantatas of J.S. Bach</a></span></i>. 2 ed. Richard D.P. Jones (Trans). 
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Oxford: Oxford University Press, 2005. 
</dd></dl>
